diplomatic_decisions = {

### Germany economical crisis ###

####################
### 1936 IC SPAM ###
####################

German_economical_crisis_I_low = {
	
		potential = {
			tag = OMG
			GER = {
				not = { has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_I }
				not = { has_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_I_low }
				not = { has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_I_low }
			}
		}
		
		allow = {
			GER = {
				total_ic = 400
				not = { total_ic = 435 }
			}
			year = 1936
			not = { year = 1937 }
			not = {
				GER = { controls = 2613 }
			}
		}
		
		effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = 85000
				set_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_I
				set_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_I_low
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "German_economical_crisis_I_low"
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
}

###############################
### Penalties removal event ###
###############################

German_economical_crisis_ends = {
	
		potential = {
			tag = OMG
			GER = {
				or = {
					has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_I
					has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_II
					has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_III
					not = { has_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_ends }
				}
			}
		}
		allow = {
			GER = {
				or = {
					and = {
						controls = 1409
						controls = 782
						controls = 2857
					}
					and = {
						controls = 1964
						controls = 2613
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		
		effect = {
			GER = {
				set_country_flag = German_economical_crisis_ends
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_I_low
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_I_medium
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_I_high
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_II_low
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_II_medium
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_II_high
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_III_low
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_III_medium
				remove_country_modifier = German_economical_crisis_III_high
				country_event = 85003
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
}

game_balance_tech_stage_1a_decision = {

	potential = {
		tag = OMG
		not = { year = 1939 }
	}
	allow = {
		not = { has_country_modifier = game_balance_tech_stage_1a_cooldown }
		date = 1936.1.1
		not = { has_global_flag = game_balance_tech_stage_1b_started }
		not = { year = 1939 }
	}

	effect = {
		OMG = { country_event = 65001 }
		#GER = { country_event = 650020 }
	}
}

buy_resources_START = {
	#major = yes
	potential = {
		not = { has_country_flag = resources_purchase }
		#ai = no
	}
	
	allow = {
		not = { has_country_flag = chromite_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = manganese_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = molybdenum_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = zinc_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = copper_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = aluminium_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = tungsten_purchase_I }
		not = { has_country_flag = nickel_putchase_I }
			or = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = blackICE
					ai = no
				}
				ai = yes
			}
	}
	effect = {
		set_country_flag = resources_purchase
		country_event = 50922
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

buy_resource_chromite = {

	potential = {
		has_country_flag = resources_purchase 	
		not = { has_country_flag = chromite_purchase_I }
		not = {
			4624 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
			6788 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
			8002 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	allow = {
		not = { has_country_flag = chromite_purchase_I }
		money = 8000
	}
	effect = {
		set_country_flag = chromite_purchase_I
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}
buy_resource_chromite_ENG = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		not = {
			THIS = { war_with = ENG }
		}
		has_country_flag = resources_purchase 	
		has_country_flag = chromite_purchase_I 	
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_SOV }
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_TUR }
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG }
		NOT = { ENG = { check_variable = { which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG" value = 2 } } }
		8002 = {
			or = {
				controller = { vassal_of = ENG }
				controlled_by = ENG
			}
		}
		not = {
			4624 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
			6788 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
			8002 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	allow = {
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG }
		money = 8000
	}
	effect = {
		money = -8000
		ENG = {
			money = 8000
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "buy_resource_chromite_ENG"
			duration = 365
		}
		ENG = { change_variable = { which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG" value = +1 } }	
		THIS = { country_event = 969700 }
		THIS = { country_event = 969701 }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}
